# Comments for Question 5, LLM=DeepSeek V3-0324

== Grader: Claude 3.7 Sonnet ==
  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=4.5)
    The writing suffers from predictable metaphors ("knots of her own unraveling") and relies heavily on abstract statements rather than concrete details. The character's transformation follows an overly neat trajectory without the messiness of authentic human change. Phrases like "dancing on the edge of madness" and "not just surviving anymore. She was dancing" feel like generic literary flourishes rather than organic expressions. The story's resolution is too tidy and formulaic, lacking the surprising turns that characterize original fiction.

  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=6.4)
    While the story avoids many AI-writing pitfalls, certain elements feel formulaic. The dialogue occasionally lacks naturalistic rhythm, particularly the statue's philosophical pronouncements. Some metaphors, like the universe built on lies, border on cliché. The story demonstrates creativity in its premise and setting, but character reactions sometimes default to expected emotional responses rather than surprising ones. The writing shows stylistic consistency and avoids purple prose, though certain phrases like "the orchard hummed with dour amusement" feel somewhat forced in their attempt at literary sophistication.

  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=6.3)
    While the story avoids most AI-writing pitfalls, there are moments where the language becomes slightly generic ("its edges resolving into something almost human"). The monster's transformation follows somewhat predictable patterns. However, the story demonstrates originality in its interpretation of the assigned elements, particularly in making the monster a forgotten program. The emotional resonance feels genuine rather than stated, especially in the understated reunion between the spy and the program.

  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=7.3)

Some phrases like "elasticize his heart" feel slightly forced, and the sister's dialogue is somewhat expositional. However, the overall narrative maintains consistent tone and avoids predictable patterns.
